streamsTopologyFromRequest;\n            } else if (group.topology().get().topologyEpoch() > topology.epoch()) {\n                log.info(\"[GroupId {}][MemberId {}] Member joined with stale topology .map(entry -> new StreamsGroupHeartbeatResponseData.TaskIds()\n                .setSubtopologyId(entry.getKey())\n                .setPartitions(entry.getValue().stream().sorted().toList()))\n                 StreamsGroupMember updatedMember) {\n        List<StreamsGroupHeartbeatResponseData.EndpointToPartitions> endpointToPartitionsList = new ArrayList<>();\n        final Map<String, StreamsGroupMember> members = group.members();\n        // Build endpoint information for all members except the updated member\n        for (Map.Entry<String, StreamsGroupMember> entry : members.entrySet()) {\n            if (updatedMember != null && entry.getKey().equals(updatedMember.memberId())) {\n                continue;\n            }\n group member. It mainly consists of\n     * three parts:\n     * 1) The member is created or updated. The group epoch is bumped if the member\n     *    has been created or updated.\n     * 2) The target assignment for the consumer group is updated if the group epoch\n     *    is larger than the current target assignment epoch.\n     * 3) The member's assignment is reconciled with the target assignment.\n     *\n     * @param context               The request context.\n     * @param groupId               The group id from the request.\n     * @param memberId              The member id from the request.\n     * @param memberEpoch           The member epoch from the request.\n     * @param createIfNotExists,\n                false\n            );\n        } else {\n            member = getOrMaybeSubscribeStaticConsumerGroupMember(\n                group,\n                memberId,\n                memberEpoch,\n                instanceId,\n                ownedTopicPartitions,\n                createIfNotExists,\n                false,\n                records\n            );\n We bump\n            // the group epoch when the member has changed its subscribed topic names or the member\n            // has changed its subscribed topic regex to a regex that is already resolved. We avoid\n            // bumping the group epoch when the new subscribed topic regex has not been resolved\n            // yet, since we will have to update the target assignment again later.\n            subscribedTopicNamesChanged ||\n            updateRegularExpressionStatus == UpdateRegularExpressionStatus.REGEX_UPDATED_AND_RESOLVED;\n\n        if (bumpGroupEpoch || group.hasMetadataExpired(currentTimeMs)) {\n            // The subscription metadata is updated in two cases:\n            // 1) The member has updated its subscriptions;\n            // 2) The refresh deadline has been reached.\n            UpdateSubscriptionMetadataResult result = updateSubscriptionMetadata(\n                group,","numLines":200,"startLine":2200,"totalLines":8823}}}

This indicates the member may have received a state update that the coordinator hasn't processed yet, creating potential inconsistency. The code throws the exception correctly but this specific condition (epoch > coordinator's known epoch) does not appear to be explicitly tested in GroupCoordinatorShardTest.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConsumerGroupHeartbeatWithMemberEpochAhead() throws Exception {\n    // Setup: Create a consumer group and add a member with epoch 5\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId = \"member-1\";\n    ConsumerGroup group = createConsumerGroupWithMember(groupId, memberId, 5);\n\n    // Act: Member sends heartbeat with epoch 10 (ahead of coordinator's epoch 5)\n    ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData request = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n        .setGroupId(groupId)\n        .setMemberId(memberId)\n        .setMemberEpoch(10);  // Epoch ahead\n\n    // Assert: Should throw FencedMemberEpochException\n    FencedMemberEpochException exception = assertThrows(\n        FencedMemberEpochException.class,\n        () -> groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), groupId, memberId, 10, null, null, -1, null, null, null, null)\n    );\n    assertTrue(exception.getMessage().contains(\"greater member epoch\"));\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**: This test exercises the conditional at line 1571-1574 in `throwIfConsumerGroupMemberEpochIsInvalid()`. The failure case (when either condition fails) throws `FencedMemberEpochException`. This validates KIP-848's fenced member recovery protocol. The subset validation at line 1578 involves a call to `isSubset()` method which has complex partition comparison logic that may not be fully covered when the subset check fails.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConsumerGroupHeartbeatWithMemberEpochBehindAndInvalidPartitions() throws Exception {\n    // Setup: Create a consumer group with member at epoch 5, previous epoch 4\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId = \"member-1\";\n    int currentEpoch = 5;\n    int previousEpoch = 4;\n\n    ConsumerGroup group = createConsumerGroupWithMemberEpochs(\n        groupId, memberId, currentEpoch, previousEpoch\n    );\n\n    // Assign partitions 0, 1, 2 to member\n    assignPartitionsToMember(group, memberId, Arrays.asList(\n        tp(\"topic-1\", 0),\n        tp(\"topic-1\", 1),\n        tp(\"topic-1\", 2)\n    ));\n\n    // Act: Member sends heartbeat with epoch 4 (matching previous epoch)\n    // but claims to own partitions 0, 1, 2, 3 (includes partition 3 not assigned)\n    List<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData.TopicPartitions> ownedPartitions =\n        Arrays.asList(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData.TopicPartitions()\n                .setTopic(\"topic-1\")\n                .setPartitions(Arrays.asList(0, 1, 2, 3))  // Partition 3 not assigned\n        );\n\n    // Assert: Should throw FencedMemberEpochException because owned partitions\n    // are not a subset of assigned partitions\n    FencedMemberEpochException exception = assertThrows(\n        FencedMemberEpochException.class,\n        () -> groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            requestContext(), groupId, memberId, 4, null, null, -1,\n            null, null, null, ownedPartitions\n        )\n    );\n    assertTrue(exception.getMessage().contains(\"smaller member epoch\"));\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**: This test exercises the conditional at line 1578-1582, specifically the case where `isSubset()` returns false. Estimated coverage increase: ~12 additional lines including `isSubset()` method and exception handling.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: FencedInstanceIdException During Static Member Replacement with Mismatched Member IDs\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 3143-3194 (getOrMaybeSubscribeStaticConsumerGroupMember) and line 1651\n\n**Description**: When a static member (identified by instance ID) attempts to rejoin with a different member ID than the previous session, the coordinator should fence the old member. The code at line 3187-3191 calls `throwIfInstanceIdIsFenced()` which validates that the new member ID matches the existing member ID for that instance. If they don't match, `FencedInstanceIdException` is thrown. This protects against concurrent static member sessions. The exception throwing path appears not to be explicitly tested in combination with the static member replacement workflow.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConsumerGroupStaticMemberRejoinWithDifferentMemberId() throws Exception {\n    // Setup: Create consumer group with static member (instance-id = \"instance-1\")\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String instanceId = \"instance-1\";\n    String originalMemberId = \"member-1\";\n\n    createConsumerGroupWithStaticMember(groupId, originalMemberId, instanceId, 1);\n\n    // Act: Same instance ID attempts to rejoin with different member ID\n    String newMemberId = \"member-2\";\n\n    // Assert: Should throw FencedInstanceIdException\n    FencedInstanceIdException exception = assertThrows(\n        FencedInstanceIdException.class,\n        () -> groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            requestContext(),\n            groupId,\n            newMemberId,      // Different member ID\n            0,                 // Rejoining (epoch 0)\n            instanceId,        // Same instance ID\n            null, -1, null, null, null, null\n        )\n    );\n    assertTrue(exception.getMessage().contains(\"instance\"));\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**: This test exercises the fencing logic at line 1651 and the sequential validation calls at line 3187-3191.
